## Tabela EstadoPais_LLP
```

  CREATE TABLE "BI1700197"."ESTADOPAIS_LLP" 
   (	"ID" NUMBER, 
	"NOME" VARCHAR2(200 BYTE), 
	"SIGLA" VARCHAR2(2 BYTE), 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_PK" PRIMARY KEY ("ID")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673"  ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_CK_01" CHECK (ID IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_CK_02" CHECK (NOME IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_CK_03" CHECK (SIGLA IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_UK_01" UNIQUE ("NOME")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673"  ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "ESTADOPAIS_LLP_UK_02" UNIQUE ("SIGLA")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673"  ENABLE
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673" ;
```

## Cidade_LLP
```
  CREATE TABLE "BI1700197"."CIDADE_LLP" 
   (	"ID" NUMBER, 
	"NOME" VARCHAR2(400 BYTE), 
	"IDESTADOPAIS" NUMBER, 
	"LATITUDE" FLOAT(126), 
	"LONGITUDE" FLOAT(126), 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_CK_01" CHECK (ID IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_PK" PRIMARY KEY ("ID")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673"  ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_CK_02" CHECK (NOME IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_CK_03" CHECK (IDESTADOPAIS IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_CK_04" CHECK (LATITUDE IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_CK_05" CHECK (LONGITUDE IS NOT NULL) ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_UK_01" UNIQUE ("NOME", "IDESTADOPAIS")
  USING INDEX PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673"  ENABLE, 
	 CONSTRAINT "CIDADE_LLP_FK_01" FOREIGN KEY ("IDESTADOPAIS")
	  REFERENCES "BI1700197"."ESTADOPAIS_LLP" ("ID") ENABLE
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "APEX_29274383503682673" ;
```
